Instead, it converts standard letters into visually similar Unicode characters defined by the Unicode Consortium.</p><p class="text-base lg:text-lg leading-relaxed backdrop-blur-sm bg-card/50 px-6 py-4 rounded-2xl border-l-4 border-primary mb-4 break-words">Unicode is an international text standard that assigns a unique code point to every character. Unicode version 15.0 includes thousands of alphanumeric style variations.</p><p class="text-base lg:text-lg leading-relaxed backdrop-blur-sm bg-card/50 px-6 py-4 rounded-2xl border-l-4 border-primary mb-4 break-words">When text is entered into www.fancyfonts.top, each character is mapped to an alternative Unicode character from supported blocks such as Mathematical Alphanumeric Symbols.</p><p class="text-base lg:text-lg leading-relaxed backdrop-blur-sm bg-card/50 px-6 py-4 rounded-2xl border-l-4 border-primary mb-4 break-words">Because these are actual characters rather than styling
